border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">学无止境</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(117, 114, 114);letter-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我的人生新阶段已经开始了，虽然不在群中学习，但是在TeacherGwen中学习已然成为一种日常，偶尔还是会打卡记录一下生活。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现如今，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">随时随地都可以作为练习的机会</strong>，举个例子，我爱看经济学的书籍，在看中文的过程中我就可以边看边翻译甚至边读英语；在看国家地理、BBC等纪录片的时候，刻意训练跟读英语。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">学习无边无界，热爱促进成长。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">en·rich / ɪnˈrɪtʃ/  VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">充实；使丰富；使饱含（某物）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This lesson will really enrich your vocabulary.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本节课将丰富你的词汇量。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> Most breakfast cereals are enriched with vitamins. 多数谷类早餐食物都加添了维生素。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">on your own 独立地， 自愿地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You really are on your own now.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你真的要靠你自己了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">on the rise 在增加；在上涨</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Near the mainland forests, temperatures are on the rise.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大陆的森林周围，气温在升高。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pro·por·tion  / prəˈpɔːʃn  ; NAmE prəˈpɔːrʃn  / NOUN</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 部份；份额</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> The proportion of regular smokers increases with age. 经常吸烟者的人口比重随年龄的增长而上升。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比例；倍数关系 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The proportion of men to women in the college has changed dramatically over the years. 近年来，这个学院的男女学生比例出现了剧变。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I am blowing things out of proportion.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我夸大事实（blow things out of proportion）了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lone·li·ness /ˈləʊnlɪnɪs/ /'lonlɪnɪs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 孤独,寂寞;人迹罕至</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And the experience of loneliness turns out to be toxic.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">孤独寂寞是有害健康的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Love is escape from our loneliness.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱是从孤单中的解脱。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mo·tiv·ate  / ˈməʊtɪveɪt  ; NAmE ˈmoʊtɪveɪt  / VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">成为…的动机；是…的原因</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> He is motivated entirely by self-interest. 他做事完全出于私利。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">推动…甘愿苦干；激励；激发</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A good biography is really, really motivating.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一本好的传记真的，真的很激励人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（就所说的话）给出理由；说明…的原因</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> Please motivate your answer to question 5. 请解释你对第 5 题所作的回答。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ten·dency  / ˈtendənsi / NOUN </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">倾向；偏好；性情</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has a strong natural tendency towards caution. 她天生喜欢小心谨慎。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">趋势 ;倾向</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is a growing tendency among employers to hire casual staff. 雇主雇用临时职员有增加的趋势。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">in·herit / ɪnˈherɪt / VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 继承（金钱、财产等）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He inherits his father's passion for jewelry.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他继承了他父亲对于珠宝的狂热。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">tol·er·ate / ˈtɒləreɪt  ; NAmE ˈtɑːləreɪt  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> 容许，允许（不同意或不喜欢的事物）  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This sort of behaviour will not be tolerated. 这种行为是不能容许的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">忍受；容忍；包容 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There is a limit to what one person can tolerate. 一个人的容忍是有限度的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有耐受性；能经受（困难条件）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> She tolerated the chemotherapy well. 她对这次化疗的耐受力很强。 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: OK, we'll see if you go<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> righ<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> late<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r o</span></span>n in the show. So, getting ba<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ck</span></span> to loneliness – the id<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ea i</span></span>s tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>becau<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> make<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s u</span></span>s feel bad, it motivates us to g<span style="color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">o o</span>ut an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> mee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>people. Some people are more likely to feel lonely tha<span style="color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">n ot</span>hers because our genes pla<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y a </span></span>ro<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">le i</span></span>n this tendency.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的，稍后我们再看你的回答是否正确。回到</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">孤独</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">的话题上来，因为孤独让我们感到很糟糕，所以这会促使我们出去和别人接触。有些人比其他人更容易感到孤独，这是因为我们的基因也在发挥着作用。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: I wonder if I inherite<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>loneliness genes.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我不知道我是否继承了孤独的基因。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: I don<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">'t</span></span> know, Neil, bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> whi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">le i</span></span>n some situations being lonely may be a good thing, because i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t e</span></span>ncourages you to be sociable, in other situations i<span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span> may be useful to tolerate – or pu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t u</span></span>p with – loneliness. Let's listen to Professor Dorret Boomsma a<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>the Vrije University in Amsterdam talk<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ing a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> this.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我不知道，但在一些情况下，孤独也许是件好事，因为它会促使你去社交，而在另一些情况下，这也许对你忍受孤独很有帮助。我们来听听阿姆斯特丹自由大学多尔特</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">布姆萨马教授的看法。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My father consoled me by telling me about the mistakes great heroes made when they were children. He told me that Mahatma Gandhi said, ‘Freedom is not worth having if it does not include the freedom to make mistakes.’ At school we had read stories about Mohammad Ali Jinnah. As a boy in Karachi he would study by the glow of street lights because there was no light at home. He told other boys to stop playing marbles in the dust and to play cricket instead so their clothes and hands wouldn’t get dirty.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为了安抚和鼓励我，父亲跟我讲了许多伟人在小时候曾犯下过错的故事。他告诉我甘地曾说：“人若不能自由地犯错，那么这自由就不值得拥有。”我们在学校里读过穆罕默德.阿里.真纳的故事。当他还是个小男孩，住在卡拉奇时，因为他家里没有电灯，会借着路灯的光线读书。他告诉其他男孩子不要在尘土里玩弹珠，改打板球，这样就不会把全身弄得脏兮兮的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我能为您效劳吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我想为我的中国之行买个纪念品。你推荐我买什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我们有许多不同种类的传统中国画。它们都是典型的中国艺术品。您看看这幅徐悲鸿绘画作品的复制品。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 徐悲鸿以画马而闻名。这幅画的原作值一百多万呢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 那么，那些汉字是谁写上去的？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 因为在中国绘画与书法密切相关，所以大多数的中国画家也都是书法家。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 作为纪念品，这幅画将是个不错的选择。您可以用它来装饰您的客厅或者书房。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 您也可以用卷轴把它卷起来，方便携带。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 要是你能给我打九折的话，我就买下这幅画。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 价格的问题，我们稍后再商量。现在，我想给您看些稍小一点的纪念品。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 您看看这些檀香扇、玉石饰品，还有其他一些手工艺品…给您的家人和朋友买一些吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 能拿一些给我看看吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 当然可以了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can I help you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'd like to buy a souvenir of my China tour. What would you recommend?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: We have many different kinds of traditional Chinese paintings. These are typical of Chinese art. Have a look at this reproduction of Xu Beihong's painting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: He's famous for his horse drawings. The original work is worth over a million yuan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Then who wrote those Chinese characters on it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Since painting is closely related to calligraphy in China, most Chinese painters are excellent calligraphers as well.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: This painting would be a good choice as a souvenir. You could decorate your living room or study with it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: You can also roll it up in a scroll that is easy to carry around.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'll take it if you can give me a 10% discount.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: We can negotiate the price later. Now I'd like to show you some of our smaller souvenirs.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Take a look at these sandalwood fans, jade trinkets and other handicrafts...Buy some for your family and friends.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Could you show me some?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Certainly.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I told him the true story, but he still thought I was throwing him off the scent.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我把实情告诉他了，可是他以为我在____________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">糊弄他</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 早读原文</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">If I learned anything when I lost everything, it's that, A, there's no wiggle room when it comes to cottage cheese expiration dates. And B, you can't get attached to material things.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. cotta</strong><span style="text-decoration: line-through;color: rgb(0, 82, 255);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ge</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cheese 后进同化；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 语调：...when I lost everything,↗  it's that, A,↗... And B,↘ ...</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">*承接下文时一般用升调，起到提示作用。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：wiggle room 〔说话或做事所留的〕回旋余地；空子</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.3900709" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdiaM4p5XghYfISBqia41jE7eONicp6lo60ocIMvXjaibia0Eibuc9RIJqo1suWthxa8JkQibtIosVm9fLlQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="423" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;height: auto !important;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We should allow for some <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">wiggle room</strong></em></span> [=flexibility] when we plan the schedule.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在计划日程时应该留出一些<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回旋的余地</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The salesman has some <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">wiggle room</strong></em></span> to reduce the price of the car.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">销售员有降低汽车价格的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回旋余地</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：there's no wiggle room 没有回旋余地</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So explain to us, where is the <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">wiggle room</strong></em></span>?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">跟我们解释一下，有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回旋的余地</strong>吗？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.620438" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdiaM4p5XghYfISBqia41jE7e0uhy2ulRqtHHWmLJSoPftoMzTS2Ru2ZYDQF1axl9r5qg0d2ic6X7OYw/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="548" style="vertical-align: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">...we should find him a little <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">wiggle room</strong></em></span>, don't you think？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们得给他点<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">回旋的余地</strong>，您觉得呢？</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. when it comes to...  谈到.../当提到...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【When it comes to...】">点击链接跳转回顾【When it comes to...】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. cottage cheese 农家干酪〔一种白色软干酪，用酸奶制成〕</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.535865" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdiaM4p5XghYfISBqia41jE7enoSrO1M1XDoWrPm0JoubUcAaoicKF6eLLrAKY2ichz1OnoSmPs6oFJFQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="474" 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. expiration dates = expiry date 到期日，失效日期</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">EXP=expiration</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">BBF=best before  〔某一日期〕前食用最佳</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">use-by date 此日期前食用；保存期</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生产日期：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">缩写"PD", 即 production date</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">或者：缩写"MFD"，即 manufacturing date。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. attach v. 把…固定，把…附（在…上）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">attached</strong></em></span> the rope securely <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>to</strong></em></span> a tree. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他把绳子牢牢地<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">系</strong>在树上。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：get/be attached to 喜欢、依恋某人/某物</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It’s easy to <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">become attached to</strong></em></span> the children you work with.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你很容易就会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">喜欢上</strong>工作中接触到的孩子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You should not<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong> get</strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> attached to</strong></em></span> money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你不应该<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">执着于</strong>金钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句</strong></span>：People<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> get attached to</strong></em></span> things.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们会对事物产生<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">依恋</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句</strong></span>：It's annoying when you<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> get attached to</strong></em></span> a book series...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">沉迷于</strong>一个系列丛书时，你会觉得很烦...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Julie better not <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong><em>get too attached to</em></strong></span> Lenny.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">朱莉最好别<strong>太迷恋</strong>连尼。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: to </strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(192, 200, 209);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(250, 250, 239);box-shadow: rgb(170, 170, 170) 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">很早以前我就发觉很多同学遇到一些问题无处求解。后来，我从2016年起在微博设立“Gwen为你答”板块，免费为大家答疑。几年来，遇到了不少共性的好问题。最近忽然想到，不如把微博上的答疑“搬”来公号，做个集合，供有同样疑问的宝子们查阅参考。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">想法不如行动，说干就干。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将近一年的答疑按照不同类别分成了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活、学习</strong>（语音 口语 听力 原版书 写作）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和推荐</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">类</strong>。暂定每周三更新。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">答疑一直在继续。如果你有什么问题，可随时来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">微博TeacherGwen</strong>私信我。只要我能帮得上忙，都会尽力解答。</span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdiaM4p5XghYfISBqia41jE7euibIyNyr17ewAibByTMFPUZWV54xicG0PCvmeIlLlKjhQXlY4icEYWclKA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="690" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">可数不可数是相对而言的。作为面包的统称（一种粮食）来讲不可数，但跳出去谈面包的“种类”、“类别”时又是可数的。很多不可数名词都是这样，要看具体的使用场景。还是那句话，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词得放到句子里，句子得放到语境里，不然学习语法毫无意义</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">很早以前我就发觉很多同学遇到一些问题无处求解。后来，我从2016年起在微博设立“Gwen为你答”板块，免费为大家答疑。几年来，遇到了不少共性的好问题。最近忽然想到，不如把微博上的答疑“搬”来公号，做个集合，供有同样疑问的宝子们查阅参考。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将近一年的答疑按照不同类别分成了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活、学习</strong>（语音 口语 听力 原版书 写作）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和推荐</strong><strong data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdiaM4p5XghYfISBqia41jE7euibIyNyr17ewAibByTMFPUZWV54xicG0PCvmeIlLlKjhQXlY4icEYWclKA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="690" normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">可数不可数是相对而言的。作为面包的统称（一种粮食）来讲不可数，但跳出去谈面包的“种类”、“类别”时又是可数的。很多不可数名词都是这样，要看具体的使用场景。还是那句话，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词得放到句子里，句子得放到语境里，不然学习语法毫无意义</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">海量阅读。</strong>泛读为主，精读为辅。语文如是，英语亦如是。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section 0%;margin-bottom: -24px;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 124.956px;height: 26.9062px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;border-width: border-box;">TeacherGwen</p></section></section></section></section></section><p><br/></</section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.intriguing: </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ɪnˈtriːɡɪŋ ; NAmE ɪnˈtriːɡɪŋ / adj. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">very interesting because of being unusual or not having an obvious answer 非常有趣的；引人入胜的；神秘的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子: She has a really intriguing personality.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">     她性格超有趣。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The food is an intriguing combination of German and French.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">该食品将德国风味与法国风味融合在一起，令人回味无穷。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.maintain</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ meɪnˈteɪn ; NAmE meɪnˈteɪn / V.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">① to make sth continue at the same level, standard, etc. 维持；保持 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：to maintain law and order/standards/a balance 维持治安；保持水平╱平衡</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> The two countries have always maintained close relations. 这两个国家一直保持着密切关系。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②to keep a building, a machine, etc. in good condition by checking or repairing it regularly 维修；保养</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：The house is large and difficult to maintain. 房子很大，难以养护。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">③to keep stating that sth is true, even though other people do not agree or do not believe it 坚持意见；固执己见 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：The men maintained (that) they were out of the country when the crime was committed. 这几个男人坚持说案发时他们在国外。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She has always maintained her innocence. 她一直坚持说她是无辜的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">④to support sb/sth over a long period of time by giving money, paying for food, etc. 供养；扶养</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：Her income was barely enough to maintain one child, let alone three.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的收入养活一个孩子几乎都不够，更不用说三个了</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.tolerate:</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈtɒləreɪt ; NAmEˈtɑːləreɪt / V.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①to allow sb to do sth that you do not agree with or like 容许，允许（不同意或不喜欢的事物）  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：Their relationship was tolerated but not encouraged.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们的关系得到了允许，但不宜鼓励。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This sort of behaviour will not be tolerated. 这种行为是不能容许的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">tolerate (sb/sth) doing/being/having sth</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：She refused to tolerate being called a liar. 她拒不接受被称为撒谎者。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②to accept sb/sth that is annoying, unpleasant, etc. without complaining 忍受；容忍；包容 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：There is a limit to what one person can tolerate. 一个人的容忍是有限度的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't know how you tolerate that noise! 我不知道你怎么能忍受那样的噪音！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">③to be able to be affected by a drug, difficult conditions, etc. without being harmed （对药物）有耐受性；能经受（困难条件）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：Few plants will tolerate sudden changes in temperature.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">很少植物经受得住气温的突然变化。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.a form of...一种，一种形式的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：Vog is a form of air pollution.火山雾是一种空气污染物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">In a way, maybe that's a form of meditation.在某种程度上，这可能是一种冥想。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Spirits became a form of money in these regions.烈酒在这些地区成为了一种货币。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.virtual：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈvɜːtʃuəl ; NAmEˈvɜːrtʃuəl / adj. [only before noun ]</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">①almost or very nearly the thing described, so that any slight difference is not important 很接近的；几乎…的；事实上的；实际上的；实质上的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：This reply is a virtual acceptance of our offer.这一回答实质上是接受了我们的建议。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The company has a virtual monopoly in this area of trade. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这家公司实质上已经垄断了这种贸易。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All virtual facing a seemingly never-ending contagion.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">实际上，我们面对着一场似乎永不停止的传染病。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">②made to appear to exist by the use of computer software, for example on the Internet （通过计算机软件，如在互联网上）模拟的，虚拟的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例子：Virtual currency was on the ropes earlier this year.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">（on the ropes :( informal) very close to being defeated 濒于失败；即将失败）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今年年初，虚拟货币的发行受到重创。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Basically, it's virtual reality circa 1955. 基本上，它在虚拟1955年左右的场景。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> one explanation is tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> probably they do not only have negative effects. feeling bad.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: or very interesting – idea. Bu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> shows <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span></em> you probably don't have those genes, Neil, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">because</em> you did feel ba<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the weekend.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这个观点很有趣。但这也说明你并没有这些基因，因为你在周末感到很糟糕。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: That's true. A<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;"> a</span></span>ctually, tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> was despite spending a lo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">f</em> ti<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">me o</span></span>n Facebook, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span></em>tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t's a </span></span>for<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">m <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">f</span></span></em> social contact. Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> doe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s all</span></span> the tweeting, messaging, an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> chattin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g on</span></span>line tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> we do ma<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ke u</span></span>s lonelier, because <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">we're</em> gettin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g ou</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> le<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ss an</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> meeting fewer people? Or do virtual connections sto<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">p u</span></span>s <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">from</em> feeling lonely?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的。尽管我花费很长时间在</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Facebook</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">上，但我还是感到孤独，虽然这也是一种社交形式。发推特、发短信、在线聊天是不是让我们更孤独了？因为我们外出的时间越来越少，见到的人也越来越少。还是说虚拟沟通让我们不再感到孤独？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: Tho<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">se <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are</em> in</span></span>triguing questions. Let's listen <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to</em> Professor Eri<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">c</span></span> Klinenberg sociologis<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> New York University an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> auth<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">or of a</span></span> boo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> livin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">g a</span></span>lone. He talk<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> this.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这是个有趣的问题。我们来听听纽约大学社会学家埃里克</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">·</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">克林南柏格教授的看法，他还写了一本有关独居的书。他谈到了以下这些。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Outside his office my father had a framed copy of a letter written by Abraham Lincoln to his son’s teacher, translated into Pashto. It is a very beautiful letter, full of good advice. ‘Teach him, if you can, the wonder of books . . . But also give him quiet time to ponder the eternal mystery of birds in the sky, bees in the sun, and the flowers on a green hillside, ’ it says. ‘Teach him it is far more honourable to fail than to cheat.’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">父亲在他的办公室外挂着一幅摹本，是林肯写给他儿子老师的一封信，已翻译成普什图语。那封信写得极好，全是极好的建议。“如果可以，请你教他书本的美好，但也给他时间，让他去思考永恒的谜题：天上的小鸟、阳光下的蜜蜂和翠绿山头上的花朵。”信里写道，“让他知道失败远比作弊光荣得多。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 早上好，先生。我能帮您什么吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 是的，我想买台电扇。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我们有很多种牌子的。您要哪个牌子的？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我要最近在电视上做广告的长城牌电扇。这种电扇看起来质量很好，即使让它一直吹也没关系。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 非常抱歉，长城牌电扇现在没货。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 真遗憾。嗯，你们什么时候再进货呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 明天我们进新货。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那我只好明天再来了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 对不起，让您白跑一趟。顺便说一下，如果您确实需要电风扇，您也许可以在我们的四川路分店买得到。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 谢谢。我去看看。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Good morning, sir. Can I help you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes, I want to buy an electric fan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: We have many brands. What kind are you looking for?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's the Great Wall fan they advertised on TV recently. It looks like it is a good-quality fan that will work even if I run it all the time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm terribly sorry. The Great Wall electric fans are out of stock now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's a pity! Well, when will you have some more?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: We're expecting some new stock tomorrow.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'll have to come again tomorrow then.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'm sorry you took the time to come here. By the way. if you need one, you might be lucky at our Sichuan Road location.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Thank you. I'll go and have a look.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The creditor drove him to the wall, which resulted in his suicide.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他因被债主_______________而自杀。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">逼得走投无路</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: o</strong></span><strong>r/we'</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);text-decoration: underline;"><strong>re i</strong></span><strong>n连读带出/r/音。</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><img class="rich_pages js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.9722222222222222" data-s="300,640" style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0,
