style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. have got to = gotta</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653538250&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=e091c0c407a37ab9972acb369203cac5&amp;chksm=f7e80707c09f8e1167f44e79f73a79f85b5bddf7a12ac965cf84d5bbf81b7d562989dbcd59fb&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接回顾 gotta">点击链接回顾 gotta</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：define XX by...  以XX来定义...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When you <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">define</strong></em></span> your life <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by</strong></em></span> what society tells you, life gets much harder. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当你用社会授予的东西来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">定义</strong>你的生活的时候，生活就变的更难了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">define</strong></em></span> yourself <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by</strong></em></span> the words you use.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你用自己的用词来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">定义</strong>自己。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：It really just means you <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">define</strong></em></span> yourself <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by</strong></em></span> what you do...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这意味着你要用你所做的来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">定义</strong>你自己...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：Do you <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">define</strong></em></span> yourself <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">by</strong></em></span> your work, your relationships, your hobbies, your passion? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你是否用你的工作，你的人际关系，你的爱好，你的热情来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">定义</strong>你自己?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-How do you <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">define</strong></em></span> “Best”？<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>-I <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>define it by</strong></em></span> the source.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-怎么<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">定义</strong>“最佳”？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-<strong>根据</strong>消息源。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6166667" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdgFRUep8tXp6GEiaicfQIYUTOS7csqUkX2jmhmXc3PauvScvca5n4Fa2ro9z8j9K6qQwmOeNcv4OLg/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《新闻编辑室》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. self-worth n. 自我价值</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Many people derive their <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-worth</strong></em></span> from their work.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">很多人从自己的工作中找到<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自身的价值</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I always feel that greeting betrays such a lack of <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self worth</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我总觉得打招呼显露出人对自己的轻视。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6222628" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdgFRUep8tXp6GEiaicfQIYUTVmrlrY1JIRHEcMbAdNosqGicoTPibIW0XRfZNDWq9AwiauuUpukdLIQrQ/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="548" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《唐顿庄园》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-XX adj. 自己的；自身的/noun. 自身的XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-esteem /self-respect  n. 自尊（心）</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You need to build your <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-esteem</strong></em></span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你需要树立<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自尊心</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-study n. 自学</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Individuals can enroll on <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-study</strong></em></span> courses.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们可以报名参加<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">自学</strong>课程。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-educated adj. 自学的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">self-made adj. 白手起家的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He was proud of the fact that he was a<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> self-made</strong></em></span> man. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他为自己<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">白手起家</strong>而自豪。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. whether or not 是否</strong></p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="list-style-type: disc;box-sizing: border-box;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">whether...or not 可以用以下几种结构：</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Whether you like it or not, ... 你喜欢也好，不喜欢也好，...</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Whether or not you like it, ... 不管你喜欢不喜欢</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Whether you like it or whether you don't, ... 不管你喜欢，还是不喜欢，...</p></li></ul><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>原句中：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">whether or not </em></span>we're in a relationship </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>=<span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">whether</em></span> we're in a relationship <span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">or not</em></span></strong><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">5. 词链儿：be in a relationship 特指在恋爱关系中</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Are you<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> in a relationship </strong></em></span>right now?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你眼下在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">恋爱</strong>吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">At the moment he isn’t <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">in a relationship</strong></em></span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">目前他的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">感情生活</strong>是空白的。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1327014" disc;box-sizing: border-box;"><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">relate v. 使有联系；</p></li><li style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p  活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">significantly  /sɪɡˈnɪfɪkəntli/ adv. 显著地；相当数量地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">significant /sɪɡˈnɪfɪkənt/ adj. 重大的；有效的；有意义的；n.象征；有意义的事物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">significant difference 明显差异</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">significant risk factor 重要的危险因素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">isolated /ˈaɪsəleɪtɪd/ adj.孤立的；分离的；单独的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">isolate  /ˈaɪsəleɪt/  vt.使隔离；使孤立 vi.隔离；孤立 adj.隔离的；孤立的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's easy to isolate yourself when you think things are going pretty well for you.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你认为一切都很好，你很容易使自己孤立起来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">critic /ˈkrɪtɪk/ n.批评家；批评者</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is not a critic, he is a little ball of bird.他哪是评论家，他简直是愤怒的小鸟。——《绝望主妇》</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">device /dɪˈvaɪs/ n.装置；仪器；策略</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The device can read a book aloud to a user.这款机器可大声朗读电子书。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">miserable /ˈmɪzərəbəl/ adj.悲惨的；痛苦的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tears came to her eyes as she thought of his hopeless, miserable life.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一想到他绝望、不幸的生活，她的眼里就充满了泪水。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">back up 支持，证明</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can find the data to back up that claim.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可以找到证据来支持这种说法</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">contagious /kənˈteɪdʒəs/ adj.感染性的；传染的；有感染力的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Laughter is contagious and appeal.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">笑是富有感染力和号召力。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">interaction  /ˌɪntərˈækʃən/  n.相互作用；互动；交往</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We like to think that our culture interaction goes both ways.我们更喜欢把文化交流视为一个双向互动的过程。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Thursday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">We jus<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> don'<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> have grea<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: blue;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> research showing that we are significantly more lonely or isolated today than we were ten or twenty or thirty years ago, which means critics<span style="color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"> who say that</span> Facebook or the internet or whatever device you carry with you, is making you lonelier and more miserable - they just don't have that much evidence to bac<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">k it u</span></span>p.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没有研究显示我们比十年前，二十年前或三十年前更孤独或更孤僻。这也就是说，批评人士认为</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Facebook</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">或网络或那些你携带的电子设备让你越来越孤独，越来越悲惨，这实际上是没有足够证据的。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: So there isn'<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">t e</span></span>nough evidence to back up – or support – the claim that social media is making us feel lonelier.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以没有足够的证据证明社交媒体让我们感到更孤独。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: No, there isn't. OK, now before <span style="color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">I give you</span> the answer to today's quiz question, Neil, did you know that loneliness is contagious?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的，没有。好了，在公布今天问题的答案之前，尼尔，你知道孤独是可以传染的吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: You mean you can ca<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">tch i</span></span>t from somebody li<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></span> cold?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你是说就像感冒一样，别人能传染给我们？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: Yes. Th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">ere are e</span></span>nvironmental factors involve<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>n loneliness too. For example, if somebody you talk to every day is always unfriendly towards you, this makes you statistically more likely to be negative in you<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">r i</span></span>nteractions with somebody else.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错。环境也是导致孤独感的因素。例如，你每天和一个对你不友好的人交流，这会让你越来越消极地对待与他人的交流。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Neil: Well, let's try and stay friendly towards each other, then, Sophie. You can start by telling me whether I got today's quiz question right!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">那让我们试着对待彼此友好一些。你对我友善可以从告诉我我今天的回答是否正确开始。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Sophie: OK. I asked: which country has the highest proportio<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>f people living on thei<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(192, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">r ow</span></span>n? Is it ... a) the US, b) Japan or c) Sweden?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好的。我问你：哪一个国家的独居人口比例最高？</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">a) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">美国</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">, b) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">日本，还是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> c) </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">瑞典</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">?</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I think everyone makes a mistake at least once in their life. The important thing is what you learn from it. That’s why I have problems with our Pashtunwali code. We are supposed to take revenge for wrongs done to us, but where does that end? If a man in one family is killed or hurt by another man, revenge must be exacted to restore nang. It can be taken by killing any male member of the attacker’s family. Then that family in turn must take revenge. And on and on it goes. There is no time limit. We have a saying: ‘The Pashtun took revenge after twenty years and another said it was taken too soon.’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我想，每个人一辈子里至少都犯过一次错误，重要的是你从中学到了什么。这就是为什么我对我们普什图习俗有着不同的看法。按习俗规定，若受委屈，我们定要采取报复手段。但这样冤冤相报，何时能了？如果家族中的男人被另一个人伤害了或杀了，他们必定要采取报复，杀死加害者家庭中的任何一个男性，以维护荣誉。这一来一往不停循环下去，没有止息。我们甚至有句谚语说：“一个普什图人花二十年复仇，其他人会说这还早着呢。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 打扰一下，我能给您再倒一杯吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好的。请倒吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 饭菜怎么样？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 很好吃。请给我点芥末好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 哦，对不起。我没有注意到这儿没有芥末了。我马上就给您拿来。顺便问一下，您还想要点其他的吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不要了，谢谢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 给您芥末。要是您不习惯用筷子的话，我们也有刀又。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 筷子就可以。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我能把盘子撤走吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 可以。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 您需要再来点馅饼吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不用了。你能把这块桌布上的碎屑清理干净吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 当然可以了。我来给您收拾干净。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Excuse me. May I refill your glass?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes. Please.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: And how is everything?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It's delicious. May I have some mustard, please?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Oh, I'm sorry. I didn't realize there was no mustard here. I'll get that for you in a minute. By the way, might I interest you in anything else?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, thank you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: And here is your mustard. If you're not used to chopsticks, we do have forks and knives.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Chopsticks are fine.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: May I remove the plates?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: OK.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Do you need any more pie?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No, but could you remove the crumbs from this cloth?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Sure. Let me clean that up for you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don’t want to make it hot for you. But I won’t tell you the true story of that till you return the letter to me.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不想________，但如果你不还给我那封信，我就不会告诉你那件事的实情。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">刁难你</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing:  听前想一想：用英语怎么说？</strong></p></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;height: auto;align-self: flex-start;z-index: 2;margin: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="white-space: pre-wrap;line-height: 1.75;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="line-height: 1.75;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 被认为是单调乏味的</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 一夜成名</strong></p><p style="margin: style="transform: rotateZ(135deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(135deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(135deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(135deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin: rgb(226, 207, 188);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最新的；最前沿的</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 17px;color: rgb(109, 109, 109);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cutting edge</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">edge，它最常用的意思是“边缘”，但是在今天要学的表达中，edge这个词的意思却是刀剑的刀刃。cutting是指：切或者是砍。cutting edge原来指锋利的刀刃，后来开始用on the cutting edge来表示在科学，研究和文学等方面比其他人都走在前面，处于最先进的地位。cutting edge就表示“最先进的；最前沿的”</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5611814" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKehGx54myoJiaQcdguROzNiatLKzuIcKrbo4RPXIAlbOEQlLYT6byoAEJsfON8JSh9xAgRHT7mLm0qQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：The software uses <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cutting edge</strong> technology.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这款软件使用了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">前沿</strong>科技。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：They were on the<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cutting edge </strong>of racing.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>他们在赛车的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最前沿</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：Her idea are more<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cutting-edge</strong> still in the world.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>她的想法在世界上还是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">很新</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在，你是不是又积累了一个关于“新”的表达。</p></section><section style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>: Uh..No, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the last thing</strong> she needs is you riding in on his perfume bottle.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链: the last thing XX  最不希望的是XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1:</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">The last person</strong> I want to see is you. 我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最不想</strong>看见你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> The last thing </strong>he needs is your help. border-box;">词链：</strong> I hope I'm not interrupting. 这个词链可以用在想插话的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> I hope I'm not interrupting</strong>.  But I really need to know where the bathroom is. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不好意思</strong>，但我真的需要知道厕所在哪里。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" </strong>be here.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这不是</strong>小孩子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该</strong>来的地方。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: rgb(226, 207, 188);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px;line-height: 1;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最新的；最前沿的</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 17px;color: rgb(109, 109, 109);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cutting edge</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">edge，它最常用的意思是“边缘”，但是在今天要学的表达中，edge这个词的意思却是刀剑的刀刃。cutting是指：切或者是砍。cutting edge原来指锋利的刀刃，后来开始用on the cutting edge来表示在科学，研究和文学等方面比其他人都走在前面，处于最先进的地位。cutting edge就表示“最先进的；最前沿的”</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5611814" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKehGx54myoJiaQcdguROzNiatLKzuIcKrbo4RPXIAlbOEQlLYT6byoAEJsfON8JSh9xAgRHT7mLm0qQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：The software uses <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">cutting edge</strong> technology.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这款软件使用了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">前沿</strong>科技。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：They were on the<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cutting edge </strong>of racing.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>他们在赛车的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最前沿</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3</strong>：Her idea are more<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> cutting-edge</strong> still in the world.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>她的想法在世界上还是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">很新</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在，你是不是又积累了一个关于“新”的表达。</p></section><section style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>: Uh..No, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the last thing</strong> she needs is you riding in on his perfume bottle.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链: the last thing XX  最不希望的是XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1:</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">The last person</strong> I want to see is you. 我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最不想</strong>看见你。</p><p style="white-space: 他<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完全不想要</strong>你的帮助。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>:  I hope I'm not interrupting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链：</strong> I hope I'm not interrupting. 这个词链可以用在想插话的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> I hope I'm not interrupting</strong>.  But I really need to know where the bathroom is. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不好意思</strong>，但我真的需要知道厕所在哪里。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong><span style="color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;">：I just wanted to tell you that I</span><strong style="color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：be supposed to XX 理应XX</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：A kid<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> is not supposed to </strong>be here.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这不是</strong>小孩子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">该</strong>来的地方。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: 0%;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;border-radius: 155%;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(239, 237, 222);min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"># </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 30px;box-sizing: border-box;">4</span></strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="color: rgb(102, 117, 149);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：It could<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> be really big for </strong>Maison Lavaux.</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：be big for XX 对XX来说是件大事；很重要</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(102, 117, 149);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句</strong>：Olympic games<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> are big for </strong>every athlete. 奥运会对每个运动员都<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">非常重要</strong>。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;color: rgb(124, 149, 124);letter-spacing: 0px;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.single-occupancy  独居</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">occupancy  / ˈɒkjəpənsi  ; NAmE ˈɑːkjəpənsi  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（房屋、土地等的）占用，使用，居住</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：the act of living in or using a building, room, piece of land, etc.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A lot of these buildings are single room occupancy.很大一部分建筑是一居室。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">扩展：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">一居室  One-bedroom， one-bedroom apartment， one-room house</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">两居室  two-bedroom</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">三居室  ...</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.arguably  / ˈɑːɡjuəbli  ; NAmE ˈɑːrɡjuəbli  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv.（常用于形容词比较级或最高级前）可论证地，按理</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：used (often before a comparative or superlative adjective) when you are stating an opinion that you believe you could give reasons to support</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is arguably the best actor of his generation. 按理他是他那一代中最优秀的演员。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.norm  / nɔːm  ; NAmE nɔːrm  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.常态；正常行为</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a situation or a pattern of behaviour that is usual or expected</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Older parents seem to be the norm rather than the exception nowadays. 人们在年龄较大时才生育子女在今天似乎成了常事，而不是个例。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.affordable  / əˈfɔːdəbl  ; NAmE əˈfɔːrdəbl  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.买得起的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">affordable prices/housing 付得起的价格；买得起的住宅</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.isolated  / ˈaɪsəleɪtɪd  ; NAmE ˈaɪsəleɪtɪd  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.孤独的；孤立的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：without much contact with other people or other countries</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Elderly people easily become socially isolated. 上了年纪的人很容易变得与社会隔绝。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.intriguing  / ɪnˈtriːɡɪŋ  ; NAmE ɪnˈtriːɡɪŋ  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.非常有趣的；引人入胜的；神秘的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：very interesting because of being unusual or not having an obvious answer</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">These discoveries raise intriguing questions. 这些发现带来了非常有趣的问题。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He found her intriguing. 他觉得她很迷人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.contagious  / kənˈteɪdʒəs  ; NAmE kənˈteɪdʒəs  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.（疾病）接触传染的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：spreads by people touching each other</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His enthusiasm was contagious (= spread quickly to other people). 他的热情富有感染力。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.edition  / ɪˈdɪʃn  ; NAmE ɪˈdɪʃn  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.（报纸、杂志的）一份；（广播、电视节目的）一期，一辑</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a particular newspaper or magazine, or radio or television programme, especially one in a regular series</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Happy to bring you this Friday's edition of CNN 10.很高兴为您带来本周五的CNN 10节目。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.guide  / ɡaɪd  ; NAmE ɡaɪd  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.指南；手册</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：a book, magazine, etc. that gives you information, help or instructions about sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a Guide to Family Health 家庭健康指南</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 95%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-left: 1px solid rgb(249, 110, 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKcaNicK4nbQaWlHrqBKiaAQ4GoErHrrfWJ5uvdUI6xtMnoxJfmtXBcUyoNSicszDSLuRoDNTKFYibjyFg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="200" style="width: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We are a people of many sayings. One is ‘The stone of Pashto does not rust in water, ’ which means we neither forget nor forgive. That’s also why we rarely say thank you, manana, because we believe a Pashtun will never forget a good deed and is bound to reciprocate at some point, just as he will a bad one. Kindness can only be repaid with kindness. It can’t be repaid with expressions like ‘thank you’.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有很多说法可以用来形容我们的民族，其中一种是“普什图的石头不会在水里变钝”。意思是说，我们既不会遗忘，也不会原谅。这就是为什么我们很少说“谢谢”，因为我们相信普什图人是不会忘记别人的恩情的，并且时候到了一定会报恩，就和一定会报仇是一样的。恩情只能用恩情来还，而不是用一句“谢谢”说说就行了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 先生，有什么需要帮忙的吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我是1021的蒂姆格林，我明天早上五点半需要叫醒电话。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的，我知道了。早上五点半，格林先生，1021房间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我想把我的叫醒时间改一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的，能告诉我您的房间号和您的名字吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我叫蒂姆，住1021房间。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 您这次想叫我们什么时间给您打电话叫醒您呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 明天早上六点半。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好的，早上六点半。我们会在那个时间准时给您打电话的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 有那么早去机场的巴士吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 有的，先生。班车每天早上五点半到晚上十点半每半小时从酒店前门发一班车。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那太好了。多谢。一定要弄准叫醒我的时间。我不想错过航班。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 没问题，先生，所有的操作都是计算机化的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What can I do for you, sir?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm Tim Green in Room 1021, and I want a wake-up call at 5:30 am tomorrow.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, I see. 5:30 am, Mr. Green, Room 1021.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I want to change my wake-up time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: OK. Could you tell me your room number and your name?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Tim, in Room 1021.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: And. when would you want us to call you this time?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: At 6:30 am tomorrow.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: OK, 6:30 am. We'll call you exactly at that time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Is there a shuttle bus to the airport that early?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, there is, sir. It leaves the hotel front door every half hour from 5 am until 10:30 at night every day.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's perfect. Thanks. Make sure you get the time right for my wake-up. I'd hate to miss my flight.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Not a problem, sir. It's all computerized.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There’s no need to worry, for your husband knows how to fob the gang off.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不用着急，你丈夫知道怎么样把那帮人__________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: the Sun</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">假如没见过太阳</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: center;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">背景音乐：</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">Tord Gustavsen、Harald Jo</span><span style="font-size: 14px;">hnsen、Jarle Vespestad - Being There</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline-block;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;margin-left: 0px;"><img data-ratio="0.685" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfqzFpL4soGrT67cwuWevuBgHcCXfUcT7kg1LaK6iaonuuB5piaZwETJeXMUvAjmjl5nQJsHiaAsN8GA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1000" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">作者：Emily Dickinson</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">翻译：蒋永强</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">朗读：Gwen</p><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Had I not seen the sun</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">假如没见过太阳</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I could have borne the shade</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我本可以忍受阴暗</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But Light a newer Wilderness</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">而今，阳光却将我的荒凉</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My Wilderness has made</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">照得更加鲜亮</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;line-height: 0;width: 8%;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1014151" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/pgC9Rudz9VUvUE94zFUGe0tW3EcqSmNNNugxQN543VLxANrGBtclBY9M6OSwUDMg4bUs7QQskngPAQzY3hfO8Q/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="424" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;padding-left: 5px;padding-right: 5px;line-height: 1.2em;margin-bottom: 2px;font-size: 18px;color: rgb(121, 121, 121);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-shadow: rgb(251, 197, 255) 2px 0px 2px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关于作者</strong></span></p></section><section style="max-width: 100%;display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;line-height: 0;width: 8%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.0375" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_gif/gDWI0uWrVSHvcvyjNUCSib0YBwdjrtGUuAwgpdte6GO7tYiadhbXiclBxNBW8GJohjw74JosibQx90G6coyJA10xow/640?wx_fmt=gif" data-type="gif" data-w="400" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">《如果我不曾见过太阳(Had I not seen the Sun)》是美国著名女诗人艾米莉·狄金森作的一首小诗，相传本诗作于1872年。该诗秉承了狄金森一贯简洁的诗风，四行两句，意蕴无穷。</span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="1.1898734" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfqzFpL4soGrT67cwuWevuBE1m0GC7emibEfI5scRibhlR7IFXso9WuuP6c3dFfJZSTrYln9xiaSQeeA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">艾米莉·狄金森（也译作狄更生）(Emily Dickinson)，美国诗人。1830年12月10日生于马萨诸塞州阿默斯特镇，出生于律师家庭。青少年时代生活单调而平静受正规宗教教育。1886年5月15日去世。她20岁开始写诗，早期的诗大都已散失。1858年后闭门不出，70年代后几乎不出房门，文学史上称她为“阿默斯特的女尼”。她在孤独中埋头写诗三十年，留下诗稿 1,775首。在她生前只有 7首诗被朋友从她的信件中抄录出并发表，其余的都是她死后才出版，并被世人所知名气极大。她的诗在形式上富于独创性，大多使用17世纪英国宗教圣歌作者艾萨克·沃茨的传统格律形式，但又作了许多变化，例如在诗句中使用许多短破折号，既可代替标点，又使正常的抑扬格音步节奏产生突兀的起伏跳动。她的诗大多押半韵。</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: auto;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);padding-right: 12px;padding-left: 12px;color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Gwen为你</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">读诗</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: left;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;margin-top: -14px;background-color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;float: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;border-radius: 100%;float: right;margin-top: -14px;background-color: rgba(231, 136, 106, 0.62);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section
